使 用 说 明
Specifications 宝盈006 V1903737
1. 本舱容表所示容量为标准温度20℃的容量，
在非20℃时应按实际情况参照下式计算：
Vt ＝ Vb × [1+3α(t - 20)]
Vt --- 经温度修正后的容量,m3；
Vb --- 舱容表所示的容量,m3；
t ----- 舱壁平均温度,℃；
α----- 舱材料的线膨胀系数；
α=.000012/℃。
1. Tank capacity in this table is based on a reference temperature of 20℃.The actual capacity should be calculated according to following formula if temperature is not based on 20℃:
Vt ＝ Vb × [1+3α(t - 20)]
Vt -- Capacity after corrected of the temperature,m3.
Vb -- the capacity shown in the tank capacity table,m3.
t ---- the average temperature of bulkhead, ℃.
α---- the linear expansion coefficient of tank material.
α=.000012/℃。

2. 空高: 液面至计量管上计量基准点的高度；
实高: 液面至计量管下计量基准点的高度；
纵倾值: 即船艉吃水值与船艏吃水值之差；
基准高度: 计量管上、下计量基准点间的
垂直高度。
3. 在容量表中， 当实高为零时的容量数据，
表示舱底量的最大值， 若舱内无液体时，
则实际货物量应为零。
4. 实高查表时，实高应加上纵倾、横倾修正
值；空高查表时，空高应减去纵倾、横倾
修正值。
2. Ullage,the distance between the free surface of the liquid and
upper reference point. Sounding,the distance between the
dipping datum point and the free surface of the liquid. Trim,
the difference between the values of draft fore and draft Aft.
Reference height, the distance between the dipping datum
point and the upper reference point.
3. In the tank capacity table, when the sounding is at the level
of zero, the capacity data will express the maximum capacity
at bottom cabin, when there is no liquid in the under-deck,
the amount of real goods is zero.
4. Sounding checkup : Trim & list correction should be added
to the sounding. Ullage checkup : Trim & list correction
should be subtracted from the ullage.
有效期至2022年12月28日！ Valid until December 28,2022.

5. 舱容计算举例：
舱号：左.1 P.1
实高：2.833m
纵倾：0.64m
横倾：右倾0.60°
舱壁温度(t)：35℃
(1) 查纵倾、横倾修正表，修正实高:
实高 2.833m
纵倾修正值① -0.002m
=
= ( + )
2.831m
横倾修正值② = ( + ) 0.005m
修正后实高 = 2.836m
(2) 用修正后的实高2.836m查舱容表，得出
20℃的舱容量：
Vb = 171.892 + 0.634/10 × 6
= 172.272(m3)
(3) 舱壁温度t=35℃时，实际舱容量为：
V35 = Vb × [1+3α(t - 20)]
= 172.272 × 1.00054
= 172.365(m3)
5. Example of tank capacity calculation
Tank NO. : 左.1 P.1
Sounding : 2.833m
Trim : 0.64m
List : 0.60° to starb'd
The temperature of bulkhead : 35℃
(1) Check trim & list Correction table to correct sounding :
Sounding 2.833m
Trim correction ① -0.002m [Page 13]
2.831m
=
= ( + )
List correction ② = ( + ) 0.005m [Page 29]
Corrected sounding = 2.836m
(2) Use the corrected sounding 2.836m to check tank capacity
table to obtain the tank capacity at temperature on 20℃:
Vb = 171.892 + 0.634/10 × 6
= 172.272(m3)
(3) When temperature of bulkhead is 35℃,the actual capcity is:
V35 = Vb × [1+3α(t - 20)]
= 172.272 × 1.00054
= 172.365(m3)
备注 Remark:
① 插值计算实高2.833m,纵倾0.64m纵倾修正值:

×(0.64-0.40)
= -2(mm)

横倾修正值= 0 + 8-(0)
1.0-0.0 ×(0.6-0.0)
= 5(mm)
① Interpolation for trim correction (Sounding2.833m,Trim0.64m):
Trim correction = -1 + -2 - (-1)

= -2(mm)

List correction = 0 + 8 - (0)
1.0 - 0.0 × (0.6 - 0.0)
= 5(mm)
